posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:Shaoxing Hotel has a nice view and good location. It is within walking distance of the north gate of Fushan Park, Cangqiao Street and Wupeng Boat City Wharf. It is only 10 minutes away from Lu Xun's former residence. Shaoxing Hotel is very large, and there are electric cars for pick-up in the park. Master Lu, who picked up at check-in, was warm and talkative. In the Fushanyue area, there is a road outside the door, and it is very convenient to take a taxi. Except for check-in and check-out, when you need to drag your luggage to the front desk, you don't need an electric car to stroll in the park at other times. When I booked the room, I was always struggling between Fushanyue (Building 3) and Building 8, which are luxurious and elegant. In the end, I chose Fushanyue. Xiao Hongshu's advice is that the recommended order of choosing a building is: Fushanyue> Building 8> Building 2/Building 5> Building 6, live in the new but not the old. I stayed here for three nights on May Day for nearly 6k. I was worried that it was a basic room. Fortunately, the room was quite large and nice to take pictures. It was good to live on the second floor. You need to swipe your card to reach the floor. At that time, I felt very safe living in the State Guesthouse. Now I think back, Fushanyue has no other security besides this. Building 8 is in the center of the park, which may be better. There is a Green Tea Restaurant on the first floor of Fushanyue, which is open to all of Shaoxing. Anyone can come in and patronize. Of course, it is convenient for us to get a number. The taste is suitable for Cantonese people and we are satisfied with the meal.

üëçüëçI like the room type I chose at Shaoxing Hotel this time. The answer was "Sorry, there are too many people borrowing quilts in Building 8 today, and there are no quilts." I went to negotiate, "You are such a big hotel and you can't get a quilt? I don't believe it. Go ask again." As a result, the quilt was delivered soon. I would like to ask, since Building 8 borrowed so many quilts that day, does it mean that your service is not in place? Is there a problem with the temperature of the central air conditioning? The sliding door between the room and the bathroom is also out of the groove, and it can't be pulled no matter how hard you pull it. The management of the breakfast restaurant is chaotic. There are no seats after entering. The lobby manager first helped us find a seat and called us over, but it was taken by another guest. The lobby manager did not communicate or apologize to us, so we had to find a seat by ourselves. After finally waiting for a seat and waiting for the waiter to clean the table, I asked a waiter who passed by for a table mat, and she shook her head, which turned out to have nothing to do with her. Finally, the waiter who came to change the table mat came. A young girl, I raised my hand to signal her, but she walked over woodenly like a robot, still holding the table mat in her hand. In the end, my husband went to get the table mat himself. I frowned at the lobby manager, and the lobby manager did not apologize at all. The next day, breakfast was on the second floor, and we shared a table with a young couple. Halfway through, the lobby manager came to apologize to one of the young ladies with a gift box and a fruit plate. I heard the reason was that the guests entered the restaurant and no one told them that they had to take a seat first, causing them to stand there with food and wait. At that time, I really wanted to ask the lobby manager, do you have to look at the person when you apologize? Shouldn't you apologize to us? Seeing you grovel to that lady, I just wanted to laugh.
I won't be superstitious about five-star hotels in the future. It's just spending money to make you unhappy. The attached picture shows the gift box that the lobby manager gave to the young lady opposite to apologize. Haha

The sleeping environment is very quiet, and the curtains are light-proof. But the room is slightly less soundproof. The Shaoxing dishes made there are authentic, the ingredients are carefully selected, and you can taste the famous local dishes. Staying in this hotel added comfort and pleasure to our journey.
